this.options = {
  ships: ships, 
  vocabulary: vocabulary,
  root_mode: "", 
  map_name: customOptions.sectorName[~~(Math.random() * customOptions.sectorName.length)],
  custom_map: "", 
  map_size: 60, 
  max_level: 8,
  maxtierlives: 5, 
  starting_ship: 801, 
  weapons_store: false,
  reset_tree: true,
  speed_mod: 1.4,
};

MapOpen();
this.tick = function(game) {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    if (game.step % 30 === 0) {
      ingameEvents();
      if (ship.crystals >= (20 * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100) * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100))) {
        ship.set({crystals: (20 * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100) * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100))-1});
      }
    }
  }
};

var events = [];
var shipCodes = [
  101, 
  201, 202, 
  301, 302, 303, 304, 
  401, 402, 403, 404, 405, 406, 407, 408,
  501, 502, 503, 504, 505, 506, 507, 508, 509, 510,
  601, 602, 603, 604, 605, 606, 607, 608, 609, 610, 611, 612,
  701, 702, 703, 704, 705, 706
];
this.event = function(event, game) {
  switch (event.name) {
    case "ui_component_clicked":
      let component = event.id;
      if (component == "regen") regenShip(event.ship);
      else if (component == "spectate") spectateShip(event.ship);
      else if (component == "switch") switchShip(event.ship);
      break;
    case "ship_destroyed":
      event.ship.custom.info = {x: event.ship.x, y: event.ship.y}; 
      if (event.ship && event.killer) {
        events.push([event.killer.id, event.ship.id]);
        setTimeout(() => {events.splice(0, 1)}, 8000);
      }
      break;
    case "ship_spawned":
      spectateShip(event.ship); 
      ShowInstructortoTeam(event.ship);
      break;
  }
};

function MapOpen() {
  game.modding.terminal.echo("[[bg;dodgerblue;]\n - Meg's Dueling - ]\n[[i;Cyan;]\nVersion: "+customOptions.version+"\nAll credits goes to LX, Megalodon, Hazard, Nébuleuse\n]");
  game.modding.terminal.echo("[[bg;Gold;]Discord Server & Commands:]");
  game.modding.terminal.echo("[[bg;black;] | ]https://discord.gg/CGktC6BsS8\n[[bg;black;] | ][[i;white;]info]\n[[bg;black;] | ][[i;white;]admin(player_ID)]\n[[bg;black;] | ][[i;white;]set(player_ID, newShip_type, crystalsAmount, newStats)]\n");
}

function regenShip(ship) {
  let max_stats;
  let max_crystals;
  clearTimeout(ship.custom.tm);
  if (ship.type === 191 || ship.type === 192) {
    if (ship.custom.init === true) interactive(ship, regen_button, "#479", "#911");
  } else {
    interactive(ship, regen_button, "#479", "#191");
    if (Math.trunc(ship.type / 100) < 7)  max_stats = 11111111 * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100); else max_stats = 0;
    max_crystals = 20 * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100) * Math.trunc(ship.type / 100);
    ship.set({shield: 999, crystals: max_crystals, stats: max_stats,invulnerable: 80});
  }
}

function spectateShip(ship) {
  let max_stats;
  let max_crystals;
  interactive(ship, spectate_button, "#974", "#191");
  if (ship.type === 192) {
    if (Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldAdminShip / 100) < 7)  max_stats = 11111111 * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldAdminShip / 100); else max_stats = 0;
    max_crystals = 20 * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100) * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100);
    ship.set({shield: 999, crystals: max_crystals, stats: max_stats, invulnerable: 80, type: ship.custom.oldAdminShip});
  } else if (ship.type === 191) {
    if (Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100) < 7)  max_stats = 11111111 * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100); else max_stats = 0;
    max_crystals = 20 * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100) * Math.trunc(ship.custom.oldShip / 100);
    ship.set({shield: 999, crystals: max_crystals, stats: max_stats, invulnerable: 80, type: ship.custom.oldShip, collider: true});
  } else {
    if (ship.type !== 192) {
      ship.custom.oldShip = ship.type;
      ship.set({shield: 999, crystals: 0, stats: 0, type: 191, collider: false});
    }
  }
}

function switchShip(ship) {
  let index;
  let next_type;
  if (ship.type === 192) {
    admin(ship.id);
    interactive(ship, switch_button, "#794", "#951");
  } else if (ship.type === 191) {
    spectateShip(ship);
    interactive(ship, switch_button, "#794", "#951");
  } else {
    interactive(ship, switch_button, "#794", "#191");
    index = shipCodes.indexOf(ship.type);
    if (index >= 0) next_type = shipCodes[(index + 1) % shipCodes.length];
    ship.custom.last_ship = next_type;
    ship.set({
      type: next_type, collider: true, shield: 999, stats: 88888888,
      crystals: 20 * Math.trunc(next_type / 100) * Math.trunc(next_type / 100)
    });
  }
}

function interactive(ship, button, colorAfter, colorTimeout) {
  clearTimeout(ship.custom.button);
  button.components[0].fill = colorTimeout;
  ship.setUIComponent(button);
  ship.custom.button = setTimeout(() => {
    button.components[0].fill = colorAfter;
    ship.setUIComponent(button);
  }, 100);
}

function ship_instructor(ship, message, character = "Lucina", delay = 0, hide_after = 0) {
  if (!ship || !message || !message.length) return;
  let instructor_func;
  if (hide_after) {
    instructor_func = function() {
      ship.showInstructor();
      ship.instructorSays(message, character);
      setTimeout(() => {
        ship.hideInstructor();
      }, hide_after * 650);
    };
  } else {
    instructor_func = function() {
      ship.showInstructor();
      ship.instructorSays(message, character);
    };
  }
  setTimeout(instructor_func, delay * 650);
}

function ShowInstructortoTeam(ship) {
  if (ship.custom.init !== true) {
    ship.custom.init = true;
    ship.custom.oldShip = 101;
    ship.setUIComponent(spectate_button);
    ship.setUIComponent(regen_button);
    ship.setUIComponent(switch_button)
    ship.set({x:0,y:0});
    switch ([0,1,2,3,4][~~(Math.random()*5)]) {
      case 0: ship.custom.instructor = "Zoltar"; break;
      case 1: ship.custom.instructor = "Klaus"; break;
      case 2: ship.custom.instructor = "Lucina"; break;
      case 3: ship.custom.instructor = "Kan"; break;
      case 4: ship.custom.instructor = "Maria"; break;
    }
    ship.custom.Time = 0;
    ship_instructor(ship, "Welcome to the offical starblast asteroid war training session!", ship.custom.instructor);
    ship_instructor(ship, "here you will only be able to access the starblast asteroid war shiptree.", ship.custom.instructor, ship.custom.Time += 4);
    ship_instructor(ship, "No waves, nothing..", ship.custom.instructor, ship.custom.Time += 5);
    ship_instructor(ship, "only you and the ships!\nenjoy!", ship.custom.instructor, ship.custom.Time += 5, 5);
  } else ship.set({x: ship.custom.info.x, y: ship.custom.info.y});
}

function ingameEvents() {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    ship.setUIComponent({
      id: "NotifBox",
      position: [55.5, 71, 24, 20],
      clickable: false,
      visible: true,
      components: [
        ...(events).map((ship, i) => [
          {
            type: "text",
            position: [0, -20 * i + 85, 50, 10],
            color: getColorRank(events[i][0])[0],
            value: getColorRank(events[i][0])[1]+game.findShip(events[i][0]).name,
            align: "center"
          },
          {
            type: "text",
            position: [26, -20 * i + 83.5, 50, 13],
            value: "☠️",
            color: "rgb(255,55,55)",
            align: "center"
          },
          {
            type: "text",
            position: [50, -20 * i + 85, 50, 10],
            color: getColorRank(events[i][1])[0],
            value: getColorRank(events[i][1])[1]+game.findShip(events[i][1]).name,
            align: "center"
          },
        ]).flat(Infinity)
      ]
    });
  }
}

function getColorRank(ID) {
  if (["Megalodon", "ƝЄ́ƁƲ☯ԼЄƲƧЄ", "LX", "HΛZΛRD"].includes(game.findShip(ID).name)) {
    switch(game.findShip(ID).name) {
      case specialNames[0]: return ["#005cb9", "\u{1F988}"]; break;
      case specialNames[1]: return ["#cf891a", "\u{1F4A0}"]; break;
      case specialNames[2]: return ["#92f8ff", "\u{1F98A}"]; break;
      case specialNames[3]: return ["#ffc900", "\u{1F3C1}"]; break;
    }
  } else return ["rgb(255, 255, 255)", ""];
}

var SAWLogo = {
  id: "SAWLogo",
  obj: "https://starblast.data.neuronality.com/mods/objects/plane.obj",
  emissive: "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/TheGreatMegalodon/Dueling-Component/main/Dueling_Component/7c8bce25332eb3cd44429961a6f793cdabdg54.png",
};
game.setObject({
  id: "SAWLogo",
  type: SAWLogo,
  position: {x: 0, y: 0, z: -14},
  scale: {x: 50, y: 30, z: 0},
  rotation: {x: Math.PI, y: 0, z: 0}
});

info = function() {
  game.modding.terminal.echo("Total amount of players: "+game.ships.length+"\n")
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\nPlayer's and their ID's:\n");
  for (let ship of game.ships) game.modding.terminal.echo("Index: " + ship.id + ", Name: " + ship.name + ", Ship type: " + ship.type + "\nCoordinates: X: " + ship.x + ", Y: " + ship.y)
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n");
}

set = function(ID,what,max_crystals,max_stats){
  if (!max_stats && max_stats !== 0) if (Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).type / 100) < 7)  max_stats = 11111111 * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).type / 100); else max_stats = 0; else max_stats;
  if (!max_crystals) max_crystals = 20 * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).type / 100) * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).type / 100); else max_crystals;
  game.findShip(ID).set({type: what, crystals: max_crystals, stats: max_stats, shield: 999, collider: true});
};

admin = function(ID) {
  let max_stats;
  let max_crystals;
  if (game.findShip(ID).type === 192) {
    if (Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).custom.oldAdminShip / 100) < 7)  max_stats = 11111111 * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).custom.oldAdminShip / 100); else max_stats = 0;
    max_crystals = 20 * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).custom.oldShip / 100) * Math.trunc(game.findShip(ID).custom.oldShip / 100);
    game.findShip(ID).set({shield: 999, crystals: max_crystals, stats: max_stats, invulnerable: 240, type: game.findShip(ID).custom.oldAdminShip});
  } else {
    if (game.findShip(ID).type === 191) spectateShip(game.findShip(ID));
    setTimeout(() => {
      game.findShip(ID).custom.oldAdminShip = game.findShip(ID).type;
      game.findShip(ID).set({shield: 999, crystals: 0, stats: 0, type: 192});
    }, 250);
  }
};
